########################################################
### EU scripted effects for new EU 1.2 voting system ###
########################################################

################################## 
### EU AI voting modifier vars ###
##################################

EU_update_AI_general_voting_modifiers = {	
	hidden_effect = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [FROM.GetTag]: 99_EU_voting_scripted_effects EU_update_AI_general_voting_modifiers"	
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = EU_member
			}
			set_variable = {	
				var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES
				value = 50
			}
			### modifiers for voting cheats
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = EU_voting_cheat_yes
				}			
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 1000 ### ai chance 					
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = EU_voting_cheat_no
				}			
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES
					value = -1000 ### ai chance
				}
			}

			### modifiers for influence of ROOT on all other EU members 
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT_influence_on_THIS_5_percent = yes
				}			
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 5 ### ai chance yes +5 no -5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT_influence_on_THIS_10_percent = yes
				}			
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 5 ### ai chance yes +5 no -5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT_influence_on_THIS_20_percent = yes
				}			
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 10 ### ai chance yes +10 no -10
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT_influence_on_THIS_30_percent = yes
				}			
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 10 ### ai chance yes +10 no -10
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT_influence_on_THIS_50_percent = yes
				}			
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 15 ### ai chance yes +15 no -15
				}
			}
			### modifiers for eurosceptic
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = {	
						check_variable = {
							var = THIS.eurosceptic
							value = 0.1
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
					}
				}			
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES
					value = -5 ### ai chance yes -5 no +5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = {	
						check_variable = {
							var = THIS.eurosceptic
							value = 0.2
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
					}
				}			
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES
					value = -5 ### ai chance yes -5 no +5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = {	
						check_variable = {
							var = THIS.eurosceptic
							value = 0.3
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
					}
				}			
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES
					value = -5 ### ai chance yes -5 no +5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = {	
						check_variable = {
							var = THIS.eurosceptic
							value = 0.5
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
					}
				}			
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES
					value = -10 ### ai chance yes -10 no +10
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = {	
						check_variable = {
							var = THIS.eurosceptic
							value = 0.7
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
					}
				}			
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES
					value = -20 ### ai chance yes -20 no +20
				}
			}															
		
			### modifiers for gov_resist
			### see focus specific modifiers
			###

			set_variable = {	
				var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_NO
				value = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES
			}		
			multiply_variable = {
				var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_NO
				value = -1
			}
		}	
	}
}

### modifier for gov_resist

EU_update_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier = {
	hidden_effect = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [FROM.GetTag]: 99_EU_voting_scripted_effects EU_update_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier"
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = EU_member
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = EU_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier_YES
				value = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = {
						OR = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 } ### conservatism
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 } ### Conservative
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 } ### Neutral_conservatism
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 0 ### ai chance yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = {
						OR = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 } ### liberalism
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 16 } ### Neutral_Libertarian
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 0 ### ai chance yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = {
						OR = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 } ### socialism
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 16 } ### neutral_Social
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 0 ### ai chance yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = {
						#OR = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 } ### Neutral_green
						#}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 0 ### ai chance yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = {
						OR = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 } ### Communist-State
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 } ### anarchist_communism
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 } ### Neutral_Communism
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 0 ### ai chance yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = {
						OR = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 } ### Nat_Populism
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 } ### Nat_Fascism
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 } ### Nat_Autocracy
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 } ### Monarchist
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 0 ### ai chance yes
				}
			}
			EU_update_AI_general_voting_modifiers = yes
			add_to_variable = {
				var = EU_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier_YES
				value = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES ### ai chance yes AI_general_voting_modifiers
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = EU_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier_NO
				value = EU_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier_YES
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				var = EU_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier_NO
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_focus_EU101_voting_modifier_YES
					value = -25 ### gov_strong_resist ### ai chance yes
				}
			}
			EU_update_AI_general_voting_modifiers = yes
			add_to_variable = {
				var = EU_AI_focus_EU101_voting_modifier_YES
				value = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES ### ai chance yes AI_general_voting_modifiers

					}

							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 } ### Nat_Fascism

			}

			}
			multiply_variable = {

				value = -1
			}
		}

### Votes ###

focus_EU001_voting_prediction_total_YES_votes = {
	set_variable = {
		var = global.focus_EU001_voting_prediction_total_YES_votes
		value = 0
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = EU_member
			NOT = {
				has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = EU_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier_YES
				value = 65
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = global.focus_EU001_voting_prediction_total_YES_votes
			value = 1
		}
	}	
}

focus_EU001_voting_prediction_total_Undecided_votes = {
	set_variable = {
		var = global.focus_EU001_voting_prediction_total_Undecided_votes
		value = 0
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = EU_member
			NOT = {
				has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = EU_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier_YES
				value = 65
				compare = less_than
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = EU_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier_YES
				value = 35
				compare = greater_than
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = global.focus_EU001_voting_prediction_total_Undecided_votes
			value = 1
		}
	}	
}

focus_EU001_voting_prediction_total_NO_votes = {
	set_variable = {
		var = global.focus_EU001_voting_prediction_total_NO_votes
		value = 0
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = EU_member
			NOT = {
				has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = EU_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier_YES
				value = 35
				compare = less_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = global.focus_EU001_voting_prediction_total_NO_votes
			value = 1
		}
	}	
}

	set_variable = {
		var = global.focus_EU001_voting_prediction_EUpopRatio_YES
		value = 0
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = EU_member
			NOT = {
				has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = EU_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier_YES
				value = 65
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = global.focus_EU001_voting_prediction_EUpopRatio_YES
			value = THIS.var_EUpopRatio
		}
	}	
}

	set_variable = {
		var = global.focus_EU203_voting_prediction_EUpopRatio_YES
		value = 0
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = EU_member
			NOT = {
				has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = EU_AI_focus_EU203_voting_modifier_YES
				value = 65
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = global.focus_EU203_voting_prediction_EUpopRatio_YES
			value = THIS.var_EUpopRatio
		}
	}	
}

focus_EU203_voting_prediction_EUpopRatio_Undecided = {
	set_variable = {
		var = global.focus_EU203_voting_prediction_EUpopRatio_Undecided
		value = 0
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = EU_member
			NOT = {
				has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = EU_AI_focus_EU203_voting_modifier_YES
				value = 65
				compare = less_than
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = EU_AI_focus_EU203_voting_modifier_YES
				value = 35
				compare = greater_than
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = global.focus_EU203_voting_prediction_EUpopRatio_Undecided
			value = THIS.var_EUpopRatio
		}
	}	
}
